vnd.unilang:пенка.html>пе́нка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pénka</span>, <span <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">phiṅgaka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span
